I have been learning a bit of Japanese. For lines 1 and 2, the use of 'kedo' (opposing 'though' grammar point) suggests that there should be some contrast between the two lines. Meanwhile, for lines 3 and 4, there is sort of lyrical wordplay going on between "tonari ni" (to be by your side) and "soba ni" (close to you). Anyway, below is my interpretation of what the song in English, with some of the grammar points and wordplays replicated:   I always make some bewilderment recently although I always screw up, causing so much trouble also So, that is why you should keep a watch on what I do Keep yourself close to me forever  Your words have been ambiguous Which means that your seriousness is not getting across From within that stoic HEART yours I want to peek inside it I might just have to melt it So then, if I use some magic, what do you think? And when I saw the translated version of the lyrics, it turned out that my guess was right.
